memory that is not being used (either unallocated or in the free list).\"),\n   212\u2192            (config, now) -> free.availableMemory());\n   213\u2192    }\n   214\u2192\n   215\u2192    private void setPartition(AppendCallbacks callbacks, int partition) {\n   216\u2192        if (callbacks != null)\n   217\u2192            callbacks.setPartition(partition);\n   218\u2192    }\n   219\u2192\n   220\u2192    /**\n   221\u2192     * Check if partition concurrently changed, or we need to complete previously disabled partition change.\n   222\u2192     *\n   223\u2192     * @param topic The topic\n   224\u2192     * @param topicInfo The topic info\n   225\u2192     * @param partitionInfo The built-in partitioner's partition info\n   226\u2192     * @param deque The partition queue\n   227\u2192     * @param nowMs The current time, in milliseconds\n   228\u2192     * @param cluster THe cluster metadata\n   229\u2192     * @return 'true' if partition changed and we need to get new partition info and retry,\n   230\u2192     *         'false' otherwise\n   231\u2192     */\n   232\u2192    private boolean partitionChanged(String topic,\n   233\u2192                                     TopicInfo topicInfo,\n   234\u2192                                     BuiltInPartitioner.StickyPartitionInfo partitionInfo,\n   235\u2192                                     Deque<ProducerBatch> deque, long nowMs,\n   236\u2192                                     Cluster cluster) {\n   237\u2192        if (topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.isPartitionChanged(partitionInfo)) {\n   238\u2192            log.trace(\"Partition {} for topic {} switched by a concurrent append, retrying\",\n   239\u2192                    partitionInfo.partition(), topic);\n   240\u2192            return true;\n   241\u2192        }\n   242\u2192\n   243\u2192        // We might have disabled partition switch if the queue had incomplete batches.\n   244\u2192        // Check if all batches are full now and switch .\n   245\u2192        if (allBatchesFull(deque)) {\n   246\u2192            topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.updatePartitionInfo(partitionInfo, 0, cluster, true);\n   247\u2192            if (topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.isPartitionChanged(partitionInfo)) {\n   248\u2192                log.trace(\"Completed previously disabled switch for topic {} partition {}, retrying\",\n   249\u2192                        topic, partitionInfo.partition());\n   250\u2192                return true;\n   251\u2192            }\n   252\u2192        }\n   253\u2192\n   254\u2192        return false;\n   255\u2192    }\n   256\u2192\n   257\u2192    /**\n   258\u2192     * Add a record to the accumulator, return the append result\n   259\u2192     * <p>\n   260\u2192     * The append result will contain the future metadata, and flag for whether the appended batch is full or a new batch is created\n   261\u2192     * <p>\n   262\u2192     *\n   263\u2192     * @param topic The topic to which this record is being sent\n   264\u2192     * @param partition The partition to which this record is being sent or RecordMetadata.UNKNOWN_PARTITION\n   265\u2192     *                  if any partition could be used\n   266\u2192     * @param timestamp The timestamp of the record\n   267\u2192     * @param key The key for the record\n   268\u2192     * @param value The value for the record\n   269\u2192     * @param headers the Headers for the record\n   270\u2192     * @param callbacks The callbacks to execute\n   271\u2192     * @param maxTimeToBlock The maximum time in milliseconds to block for buffer memory to be available\n   272\u2192     * @param nowMs The current time, in milliseconds\n   273\u2192     * @param cluster The cluster metadata\n   274\u2192     */\n   275\u2192    public RecordAppendResult append(String topic,\n   276\u2192                                     int partition,\n   277\u2192                                     long timestamp,\n   278\u2192                                     byte[] key,\n   279\u2192                                     byte[] value,\n   280\u2192                                     Header[] headers,\n   281\u2192                                     AppendCallbacks callbacks,\n   282\u2192                                     long maxTimeToBlock,\n   283\u2192                                     long nowMs,\n   284\u2192                                     Cluster cluster) throws InterruptedException {\n   285\u2192        TopicInfo topicInfo = topicInfoMap.computeIfAbsent(topic, k -> new TopicInfo(createBuiltInPartitioner(logContext, k, batchSize)));\n   286\u2192\n   287\u2192        // We keep track of the number of appending thread to make sure we do not miss batches in\n   288\u2192        // abortIncompleteBatches().\n   289\u2192        appendsInProgress.incrementAndGet();\n   290\u2192        ByteBuffer buffer = null;\n   291\u2192        if (headers == null) headers = Record.EMPTY_HEADERS;\n   292\u2192        try {\n   293\u2192            // Loop to retry in case we encounter partitioner's race conditions.\n   294\u2192            while (true) {\n   295\u2192                // If the message doesn't have any partition affinity, so we pick a partition based on the broker\n   296\u2192                // availability and performance.  Note, that here we peek current partition before we hold the\n   297\u2192                // deque lock, so we'll need to make sure that it's not changed while we were waiting for the\n   298\u2192                // deque lock.\n   299\u2192                final BuiltInPartitioner.StickyPartitionInfo partitionInfo;\n   300\u2192                final int effectivePartition;\n   301\u2192                if (partition == RecordMetadata.UNKNOWN_PARTITION) {\n   302\u2192                    partitionInfo = topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.peekCurrentPartitionInfo(cluster);\n   303\u2192                    effectivePartition = partitionInfo.partition();\n   304\u2192                } else {\n   305\u2192                    partitionInfo = null;\n   306\u2192                    effectivePartition = partition;\n   307\u2192                }\n   308\u2192\n   309\u2192                // Now that we know the effective partition, let the caller know.\n   310\u2192                setPartition(callbacks, effectivePartition);\n   311\u2192\n   312\u2192                // check if we have an in-progress batch\n   313\u2192                Deque<ProducerBatch> dq = topicInfo.batches.computeIfAbsent(effectivePartition, k -> new ArrayDeque<>());\n   314\u2192                synchronized (dq) {\n   315\u2192                    // After taking the lock, validate that the partition hasn't changed and retry.\n   316\u2192                    if (partitionChanged(topic, topicInfo, partitionInfo, dq, nowMs, cluster))\n   317\u2192                        continue;\n   318\u2192\n   319\u2192                    RecordAppendResult appendResult = tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers, callbacks, dq, nowMs);\n   320\u2192                    if (appendResult != null) {\n   321\u2192                        // If queue has incomplete batches we disable switch (see comments in updatePartitionInfo).\n   322\u2192                        boolean enableSwitch = allBatchesFull(dq);\n   323\u2192                        topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.updatePartitionInfo(partitionInfo, appendResult.appendedBytes, cluster, enableSwitch);\n   324\u2192                        return appendResult;\n   325\u2192                    }\n   326\u2192                }\n   327\u2192\n   328\u2192                if (buffer == null) {\n   329\u2192                    int size = Math.max(this.batchSize, AbstractRecords.estimateSizeInBytesUpperBound(\n   330\u2192                            RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression.type(), key, value, headers));\n   331\u2192                    log.trace(\"Allocating a new {} byte message buffer for topic {} partition {} with remaining timeout {}ms\", size, topic, effectivePartition, maxTimeToBlock);\n   332\u2192                    // This call may block if we exhausted buffer space.\n   333\u2192                    buffer = free.allocate(size, maxTimeToBlock);\n   334\u2192                    // Update the current time in case the buffer allocation blocked above.\n   335\u2192                    // NOTE: getting time may be expensive, so calling it under a lock\n   336\u2192                    // should be avoided.\n   337\u2192                    nowMs = time.milliseconds();\n   338\u2192                }\n   339\u2192\n   340\u2192                synchronized (dq) {\n   341\u2192                    // After taking the lock, validate that the partition hasn't changed and retry.\n   342\u2192                    if (partitionChanged(topic, topicInfo, partitionInfo, dq, nowMs, cluster))\n   343\u2192                        continue;\n   344\u2192\n   345\u2192                    RecordAppendResult appendResult = appendNewBatch(topic, effectivePartition, dq, timestamp, key, value, headers, callbacks, buffer, nowMs);\n   346\u2192                    // Set buffer to null, so that deallocate doesn't return it back to free pool, since it's used in the batch.\n   347\u2192                    if (appendResult.newBatchCreated)\n   348\u2192                        buffer = null;\n   349\u2192                    // If queue has incomplete batches we disable switch (see comments in updatePartitionInfo).\n   350\u2192                    boolean enableSwitch = allBatchesFull(dq);\n   351\u2192                    topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.updatePartitionInfo(partitionInfo, appendResult.appendedBytes, cluster, enableSwitch);\n   352\u2192                    return appendResult;\n   353\u2192                }\n   354\u2192            }\n   355\u2192        } finally {\n   356\u2192            free.deallocate(buffer);\n   357\u2192            appendsInProgress.decrementAndGet();\n   358\u2192        }\n   359\u2192    }\n   360\u2192\n   361\u2192    /**\n   362\u2192     * Append a new batch to the queue\n   363\u2192     *\n   364\u2192     * @param topic The topic\n   365\u2192     * @param partition The partition (cannot be RecordMetadata.UNKNOWN_PARTITION)\n   366\u2192     * @param dq The queue\n   367\u2192     * @param timestamp The timestamp of the record\n   368\u2192     * @param key The key for the record\n   369\u2192     * @param value The value for the record\n   370\u2192     * @param headers the Headers for the record\n   371\u2192     * @param callbacks The callbacks to execute\n   372\u2192     * @param buffer The buffer for the new batch\n   373\u2192     * @param nowMs The current time, in milliseconds\n   374\u2192     */\n   375\u2192    private RecordAppendResult appendNewBatch(String topic,\n   376\u2192                                              int partition,\n   377\u2192                                              Deque<ProducerBatch> dq,\n   378\u2192                                              long timestamp,\n   379\u2192                                              byte[] key,\n   380\u2192                                              byte[] value,\n   381\u2192                                              Header[] headers,\n   382\u2192                                              AppendCallbacks callbacks,\n   383\u2192                                              ByteBuffer buffer,\n   384\u2192                                              long nowMs) {\n   385\u2192        assert partition != RecordMetadata.UNKNOWN_PARTITION;\n   386\u2192\n   387\u2192        RecordAppendResult appendResult = tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers, callbacks, dq, nowMs);\n   388\u2192        if (appendResult != null) {\n   389\u2192            // Somebody else found us a batch, return the one we waited for! Hopefully this doesn't happen often...\n   390\u2192            return appendResult;\n   391\u2192        }\n   392\u2192\n   393\u2192        MemoryRecordsBuilder recordsBuilder = recordsBuilder(buffer);\n   394\u2192        ProducerBatch batch = new ProducerBatch(new TopicPartition(topic, partition), recordsBuilder, nowMs);\n   395\u2192        FutureRecordMetadata future = Objects.requireNonNull(batch.tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers,\n   396\u2192                callbacks, nowMs));\n   397\u2192\n   398\u2192        dq.addLast(batch);\n   399\u2192        incomplete.add(batch);\n   400\u2192\n   401\u2192        return new RecordAppendResult(future, dq.size() > 1 || batch.isFull(), true, batch.estimatedSizeInBytes());\n   402\u2192    }\n   403\u2192\n   404\u2192    private MemoryRecordsBuilder recordsBuilder(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n   405\u2192        return MemoryRecords.builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, TimestampType.CREATE_TIME, 0L);\n   406\u2192    }\n   407\u2192\n   408\u2192    /**\n   409\u2192     * Check if all batches in the queue are full.\n   410\u2192     */\n   411\u2192    private boolean allBatchesFull(Deque<ProducerBatch> deque) {\n   412\u2192        // Only the last batch may be incomplete, so we just check that.\n   413\u2192        ProducerBatch last = deque.peekLast();\n   414\u2192        return last == null || last.isFull();\n   415\u2192    }\n   416\u2192\n   417\u2192     /**\n   418\u2192     *  Try to append to a ProducerBatch.\n   419\u2192     *\n   420\u2192     *  If it is full, we return null and a new batch is created. We also close the batch for record appends to free up\n   421\u2192     *  resources like compression buffers. The batch will be fully closed (ie. the record batch headers will be written\n   422\u2192     *  and memory records built) in one of the following cases (whichever comes first): right before send,\n   423\u2192     *  if it is expired, or when the producer is closed.\n   424\u2192     */\n   425\u2192    private RecordAppendResult tryAppend(long timestamp, byte[] key, byte[] value, Header[] headers,\n   426\u2192                                         Callback callback, Deque<ProducerBatch> deque, long nowMs) {\n   427\u2192        if (closed)\n   428\u2192            throw new KafkaException(\"Producer closed while send in progress\");\n   429\u2192        ProducerBatch last = deque.peekLast();\n   430\u2192        if (last != null) {\n   431\u2192            int initialBytes = last.estimatedSizeInBytes();\n   432\u2192            FutureRecordMetadata future = last.tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers, callback, nowMs);\n   433\u2192            if (future == null) {\n   434\u2192                last.closeForRecordAppends();\n   435\u2192            } else {\n   436\u2192                int appendedBytes = last.estimatedSizeInBytes() - initialBytes;\n   437\u2192                return new RecordAppendResult(future, deque.size() > 1 || last.isFull(), false, appendedBytes);\n   438\u2192            }\n   439\u2192        }\n   440\u2192        return null;\n   441\u2192    }\n   442\u2192\n   443\u2192    private boolean isMuted(TopicPartition tp) {\n   444\u2192        return muted.contains(tp);\n   445\u2192    }\n   446\u2192\n   447\u2192    public void resetNextBatchExpiryTime() {\n   448\u2192        nextBatchExpiryTimeMs = Long.MAX_VALUE;\n   449\u2192    }\n   450\u2192\n   451\u2192    public void maybeUpdateNextBatchExpiryTime(ProducerBatch batch) {\n   452\u2192        if (batch.createdMs + deliveryTimeoutMs  > 0) {\n   453\u2192            // the non-negative check is to guard us against potential overflow due to setting\n   454\u2192            // a large value for deliveryTimeoutMs\n   455\u2192            nextBatchExpiryTimeMs = Math.min(nextBatchExpiryTimeMs, batch.createdMs + deliveryTimeoutMs);\n   456\u2192        } else {\n   457\u2192            log.warn(\"Skipping next batch expiry time update due to addition overflow: \"\n   458\u2192                + \"batch.createMs={}, deliveryTimeoutMs={}\", batch.createdMs, deliveryTimeoutMs);\n   459\u2192        }\n   460\u2192    }\n   461\u2192\n   462\u2192    /**\n   463\u2192     * Get a list of batches which have been sitting in the accumulator too long and need to be expired.\n   464\u2192     */\n   465\u2192    public List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches(long now) {\n   466\u2192        List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = new ArrayList<>();\n   467\u2192        for (TopicInfo topicInfo : topicInfoMap.values()) {\n   468\u2192            for (Deque<ProducerBatch> deque : topicInfo.batches.values()) {\n   469\u2192                // expire the batches in the order of sending\n   470\u2192                synchronized (deque) {\n   471\u2192                    while (!deque.isEmpty()) {\n   472\u2192                        ProducerBatch batch = deque.getFirst();\n   473\u2192                        if (batch.hasReachedDeliveryTimeout(deliveryTimeoutMs, now)) {\n   474\u2192                            deque.poll();\n   475\u2192                            batch.abortRecordAppends();\n   476\u2192                            expiredBatches.add(batch);\n   477\u2192                        } else {\n   478\u2192                            maybeUpdateNextBatchExpiryTime(batch);\n   479\u2192                            break;\n   480\u2192                        }\n   481\u2192                    }\n   482\u2192                }\n   483\u2192            }\n   484\u2192        }\n   485\u2192        return expiredBatches;\n   486\u2192    }\n   487\u2192\n   488\u2192    public long getDeliveryTimeoutMs() {\n   489\u2192        return deliveryTimeoutMs;\n   490\u2192    }\n   491\u2192\n   492\u2192    /**\n   493\u2192     * Re-enqueue the given record batch in the accumulator. In Sender.completeBatch method, we check\n   494\u2192     * whether the batch has reached deliveryTimeoutMs or not. Hence we do not do the delivery timeout check here.\n   495\u2192     */\n   496\u2192    public void reenqueue(ProducerBatch batch, long now) {\n   497\u2192        batch.reenqueued(now);\n   498\u2192        Deque<ProducerBatch> deque = getOrCreateDeque(batch.topicPartition);\n   499\u2192        synchronized (deque) {\n   500\u2192            if (transactionManager != null)\n   501\u2192                insertInSequenceOrder(deque, batch);\n   502\u2192            else\n   503\u2192                deque.addFirst(batch);\n   504\u2192        }\n   505\u2192    }\n   506\u2192\n   507\u2192    /**\n   508\u2192     * Split the big batch that has been rejected and reenqueue the split batches in to the accumulator.\n   509\u2192     * @return the number of split batches.\n   510\u2192     */\n   511\u2192    public int splitAndReenqueue(ProducerBatch bigBatch) {\n   512\u2192        // Reset the estimated compression ratio to the initial value or the big batch compression ratio, whichever\n   513\u2192        // is bigger. There are several different ways to do the reset. We chose the most conservative one to ensure\n   514\u2192        // the split doesn't happen too often.\n   515\u2192        CompressionRatioEstimator.setEstimation(bigBatch.topicPartition.topic(), compression.type(),\n   516\u2192                                                Math.max(1.0f, (float) bigBatch.compressionRatio()));\n   517\u2192        Deque<ProducerBatch> dq = bigBatch.split(this.batchSize);\n   518\u2192        int numSplitBatches = dq.size();\n   519\u2192        Deque<ProducerBatch> partitionDequeue = getOrCreateDeque(bigBatch.topicPartition);\n   520\u2192        while (!dq.isEmpty()) {\n   521\u2192            ProducerBatch batch = dq.pollLast();\n   522\u2192            incomplete.add(batch);\n   523\u2192            // We treat the newly split batches as if they are not even tried.\n   524\u2192            synchronized (partitionDequeue) {\n   525\u2192                if (transactionManager != null) {\n   526\u2192                    // We should track the newly created batches since they already have assigned sequences.\n   527\u2192                    transactionManager.addInFlightBatch(batch);\n   528\u2192                    insertInSequenceOrder(partitionDequeue, batch);\n   529\u2192                } else {\n   530\u2192                    partitionDequeue.addFirst(batch);\n   531\u2192                }\n   532\u2192            }\n   533\u2192        }\n   534\u2192        return numSplitBatches;\n   535\u2192    }\n   536\u2192\n   537\u2192    // We will have to do extra work to ensure the queue is in order when requests are being retried and there are\n   538\u2192    // multiple requests in flight to that partition. If the first in flight request fails to append, then all the\n   539\u2192    // subsequent in flight requests will also fail because the sequence numbers will not be accepted.\n   540\u2192    //\n   541\u2192    // Further, once batches are being retried, we are reduced to a single in flight request for that partition. So when\n   542\u2192    // the subsequent batches come back in sequence order, they will have to be placed further back in the queue.\n   543\u2192    //\n   544\u2192    // Note that this assumes that all the batches in the queue which have an assigned sequence also have the current\n   545\u2192    // producer id. We will not attempt to reorder messages if the producer id has changed, we will throw an\n   546\u2192    // IllegalStateException instead.\n   547\u2192    private void insertInSequenceOrder(Deque<ProducerBatch> deque, ProducerBatch batch) {\n   548\u2192        // When we are re-enqueueing and have enabled idempotence, the re-enqueued batch must always have a sequence.\n   549\u2192        if (batch.baseSequence() == RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE)\n   550\u2192            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Trying to re-enqueue a batch which doesn't have a sequence even \" +\n   551\u2192                \"though idempotency is enabled.\");\n   552\u2192\n   553\u2192        if (!transactionManager.hasInflightBatches(batch.topicPartition))\n   554\u2192            throw new IllegalStateException(\"We are re-enqueueing a batch which is not tracked as part of the in flight \" +\n   555\u2192                \"requests. batch.topicPartition: \" + batch.topicPartition + \"; batch.baseSequence: \" + batch.baseSequence());\n   556\u2192\n   557\u2192        ProducerBatch firstBatchInQueue = deque.peekFirst();\n   558\u2192        if (firstBatchInQueue != null && firstBatchInQueue.hasSequence() && firstBatchInQueue.baseSequence() < batch.baseSequence()) {\n   559\u2192            // The incoming batch can't be inserted at the front of the queue without violating the sequence ordering.\n   560\u2192            // This means that the incoming batch should be placed somewhere further back.\n   561\u2192            // We need to find the right place for the incoming batch and insert it there.\n   562\u2192            // We will only enter this branch if we have multiple inflights sent to different brokers and we need to retry\n   563\u2192            // the inflight batches.\n   564\u2192            //\n   565\u2192            // Since we reenqueue exactly one batch a time and ensure that the queue is ordered by sequence always, it\n   566\u2192            // is a simple linear scan of a subset of the in flight batches to find the right place in the queue each time.\n   567\u2192            List<ProducerBatch> orderedBatches = new ArrayList<>();\n   568\u2192            while (deque.peekFirst() != null && deque.peekFirst().hasSequence() && deque.peekFirst().baseSequence() < batch.baseSequence())\n   569\u2192                orderedBatches.add(deque.pollFirst());\n   570\u2192\n   571\u2192            log.debug(\"Reordered incoming batch with sequence {} for partition {}. It was placed in the queue at \" +\n   572\u2192                \"position {}\", batch.baseSequence(), batch.topicPartition, orderedBatches.size());\n   573\u2192            // Either we have reached a point where there are batches without a sequence (ie. never been drained\n   574\u2192            // and are hence in order by default), or the batch at the front of the queue has a sequence greater\n   575\u2192            // than the incoming batch. This is the right place to add the incoming batch.\n   576\u2192            deque.addFirst(batch);\n   577\u2192\n   578\u2192            // Now we have to re insert the previously queued batches in the right order.\n   579\u2192            for (int i = orderedBatches.size() - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\n   580\u2192                deque.addFirst(orderedBatches.get(i));\n   581\u2192            }\n   582\u2192\n   583\u2192            // At this point, the incoming batch has been queued in the correct place according to its sequence.\n   584\u2192        } else {\n   585\u2192            deque.addFirst(batch);\n   586\u2192        }\n   587\u2192    }\n   588\u2192\n   589\u2192    /**\n   590\u2192     * Add the leader to the ready nodes if the batch is ready\n   591\u2192     *\n   592\u2192     * @param exhausted 'true' is the buffer pool is exhausted\n   593\u2192     * @param part The partition\n   594\u2192     * @param leader The leader for the partition\n   595\u2192     * @param waitedTimeMs How long batch waited\n   596\u2192     * @param backingOff Is backing off\n   597\u2192     * @param backoffAttempts Number of attempts for calculating backoff delay\n   598\u2192     * @param full Is batch full\n   599\u2192     * @param nextReadyCheckDelayMs The delay for next check\n   600\u2192     * @param readyNodes The set of ready nodes (to be filled in)\n   601\u2192     * @return The delay for next check\n   602\u2192     */\n   603\u2192    private long batchReady(boolean exhausted, TopicPartition part, Node leader,\n   604\u2192                            long waitedTimeMs, boolean backingOff, int backoffAttempts,\n   605\u2192                            boolean full, long nextReadyCheckDelayMs, Set<Node> readyNodes) {\n   606\u2192        if (!readyNodes.contains(leader) && !isMuted(part)) {\n   607\u2192            long timeToWaitMs = backingOff ? retryBackoff.backoff(backoffAttempts > 0 ? backoffAttempts - 1 : 0) : lingerMs;\n   608\u2192            boolean expired = waitedTimeMs >= timeToWaitMs;\n   609\u2192            boolean transactionCompleting = transactionManager != null && transactionManager.isCompleting();\n   610\u2192            boolean sendable = full\n   611\u2192                    || expired\n   612\u2192                    || exhausted\n   613\u2192                    || closed\n   614\u2192                    || flushInProgress()\n   615\u2192                    || transactionCompleting;\n   616\u2192            if (sendable && !backingOff) {\n   617\u2192                readyNodes.add(leader);\n   618\u2192            } else {\n   619\u2192                long timeLeftMs = Math.max(timeToWaitMs - waitedTimeMs, 0);\n   620\u2192                // Note that this results in a conservative estimate since an un-sendable partition may have\n   621\u2192                // a leader that will later be found to have sendable data. However, this is good enough\n   622\u2192                // since we'll just wake up and then sleep again for the remaining time.\n   623\u2192                nextReadyCheckDelayMs = Math.min(timeLeftMs, nextReadyCheckDelayMs);\n   624\u2192            }\n   625\u2192        }\n   626\u2192        return nextReadyCheckDelayMs;\n   627\u2192    }\n   628\u2192\n   629\u2192    /**\n   630\u2192     * Iterate over partitions to see which one have batches ready and collect leaders of those\n   631\u2192     * partitions into the set of ready nodes.  If partition has no leader, add the topic to the set\n   632\u2192     * of topics with no leader.  This function also calculates stats for adaptive partitioning.\n   633\u2192     *\n   634\u2192     * @param metadataSnapshot      The cluster metadata\n   635\u2192     * @param nowMs                 The current time\n   636\u2192     * @param topic                 The topic\n   637\u2192     * @param topicInfo             The topic info\n   638\u2192     * @param nextReadyCheckDelayMs The delay for next check\n   639\u2192     * @param readyNodes            The set of ready nodes (to be filled in)\n   640\u2192     * @param unknownLeaderTopics   The set of topics with no leader (to be filled in)\n   641\u2192     * @return The delay for next check\n   642\u2192     */\n   643\u2192    private long partitionReady(MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot, long nowMs, String topic,\n   644\u2192                                TopicInfo topicInfo,\n   645\u2192                                long nextReadyCheckDelayMs, Set<Node> readyNodes, Set<String> unknownLeaderTopics) {\n   646\u2192        ConcurrentMap<Integer, Deque<ProducerBatch>> batches = topicInfo.batches;\n   647\u2192        // Collect the queue sizes for available partitions to be used in adaptive partitioning.\n   648\u2192        int[] queueSizes = null;\n   649\u2192        int[] partitionIds = null;\n   650\u2192        if (enableAdaptivePartitioning && batches.size() >= metadataSnapshot.cluster().partitionsForTopic(topic).size()) {\n   651\u2192            // We don't do adaptive partitioning until we scheduled at least a batch for all\n   652\u2192            // partitions (i.e. we have the corresponding entries in the batches map), we just\n   653\u2192            // do uniform.  The reason is that we build queue sizes from the batches map,\n   654\u2192            // and if an entry is missing in the batches map, then adaptive partitioning logic\n   655\u2192            // won't know about it and won't switch to it.\n   656\u2192            queueSizes = new int[batches.size()];\n   657\u2192            partitionIds = new int[queueSizes.length];\n   658\u2192        }\n   659\u2192\n   660\u2192        int queueSizesIndex = -1;\n   661\u2192        boolean exhausted = this.free.queued() > 0;\n   662\u2192        for (Map.Entry<Integer, Deque<ProducerBatch>> entry : batches.entrySet()) {\n   663\u2192            TopicPartition part = new TopicPartition(topic, entry.getKey());\n   664\u2192            // Advance queueSizesIndex so that we properly index available\n   665\u2192            // partitions.  Do it here so that it's done for all code paths.\n   666\u2192\n   667\u2192            Node leader = metadataSnapshot.cluster().leaderFor(part);\n   668\u2192            if (leader != null && queueSizes != null) {\n   669\u2192                ++queueSizesIndex;\n   670\u2192                assert queueSizesIndex < queueSizes.length;\n   671\u2192                partitionIds[queueSizesIndex] = part.partition();\n   672\u2192            }\n   673\u2192\n   674\u2192            Deque<ProducerBatch> deque = entry.getValue();\n   675\u2192\n   676\u2192            final long waitedTimeMs;\n   677\u2192            final boolean backingOff;\n   678\u2192            final int backoffAttempts;\n   679\u2192            final int dequeSize;\n   680\u2192            final boolean full;\n   681\u2192\n   682\u2192            OptionalInt leaderEpoch = metadataSnapshot.leaderEpochFor(part);\n   683\u2192\n   684\u2192            // This loop is especially hot with large partition counts. So -\n   685\u2192\n   686\u2192            // 1. We should avoid code that increases synchronization between application thread calling\n   687\u2192            // send(), and background thread running runOnce(), see https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-16226\n   688\u2192\n   689\u2192            // 2. We are careful to only perform the minimum required inside the\n   690\u2192            // synchronized block, as this lock is also used to synchronize producer threads\n   691\u2192            // attempting to append() to a partition/batch.\n   692\u2192\n   693\u2192            synchronized (deque) {\n   694\u2192                // Deques are often empty in this path, esp with large partition counts,\n   695\u2192                // so we exit early if we can.\n   696\u2192                ProducerBatch batch = deque.peekFirst();\n   697\u2192                if (batch == null) {\n   698\u2192                    continue;\n   699\u2192                }\n   700\u2192\n   701\u2192                waitedTimeMs = batch.waitedTimeMs(nowMs);\n   702\u2192                batch.maybeUpdateLeaderEpoch(leaderEpoch);\n   703\u2192                backingOff = shouldBackoff(batch.hasLeaderChangedForTheOngoingRetry(), batch, waitedTimeMs);\n   704\u2192                backoffAttempts = batch.attempts();\n   705\u2192                dequeSize = deque.size();\n   706\u2192                full = dequeSize > 1 || batch.isFull();\n   707\u2192            }\n   708\u2192\n   709\u2192            if (leader == null) {\n   710\u2192                // This is a partition for which leader is not known, but messages are available to send.\n   711\u2192                // Note that entries are currently not removed from batches when deque is empty.\n   712\u2192                unknownLeaderTopics.add(part.topic());\n   713\u2192            } else {\n   714\u2192                if (queueSizes != null)\n   715\u2192                    queueSizes[queueSizesIndex] = dequeSize;\n   716\u2192                if (partitionAvailabilityTimeoutMs > 0) {\n   717\u2192                    // Check if we want to exclude the partition from the list of available partitions\n   718\u2192                    // if the broker hasn't responded for some time.\n   719\u2192                    NodeLatencyStats nodeLatencyStats = nodeStats.get(leader.id());\n   720\u2192                    if (nodeLatencyStats != null) {\n   721\u2192                        // NOTE: there is no synchronization between reading metrics,\n   722\u2192                        // so we read ready time first to avoid accidentally marking partition\n   723\u2192                        // unavailable if we read while the metrics are being updated.\n   724\u2192                        long readyTimeMs = nodeLatencyStats.readyTimeMs;\n   725\u2192                        if (readyTimeMs - nodeLatencyStats.drainTimeMs > partitionAvailabilityTimeoutMs)\n   726\u2192                            --queueSizesIndex;\n   727\u2192                    }\n   728\u2192                }\n   729\u2192\n   730\u2192                nextReadyCheckDelayMs = batchReady(exhausted, part, leader, waitedTimeMs, backingOff,\n   731\u2192                    backoffAttempts, full, nextReadyCheckDelayMs, readyNodes);\n   732\u2192            }\n   733\u2192        }\n   734\u2192\n   735\u2192        // We've collected the queue sizes for partitions of this topic, now we can calculate\n   736\u2192        // load stats.  NOTE: the stats are calculated in place, modifying the\n   737\u2192        // queueSizes array.\n   738\u2192        topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.updatePartitionLoadStats(queueSizes, partitionIds, queueSizesIndex + 1);\n   739\u2192        return nextReadyCheckDelayMs;\n   740\u2192    }\n   741\u2192\n   742\u2192    /**\n   743\u2192     * Get a list of nodes whose partitions are ready to be sent, and the earliest time at which any non-sendable\n   744\u2192     * partition will be ready; Also return the flag for whether there are any unknown leaders for the accumulated\n   745\u2192     * partition batches.\n   746\u2192     * <p>\n   747\u2192     * A destination node is ready to send data if:\n   748\u2192     * <ol>\n   749\u2192     * <li>There is at least one partition that is not backing off its send\n   750\u2192     * <li><b>and</b> those partitions are not muted (to prevent reordering if\n   751\u2192     *   {@value org.apache.kafka.clients.producer.ProducerConfig#MAX_IN_FLIGHT_REQUESTS_PER_CONNECTION}\n   752\u2192     *   is set to one)</li>\n   753\u2192     * <li><b>and <i>any</i></b> of the following are true</li>\n   754\u2192     * <ul>\n   755\u2192     *     <li>The record set is full</li>\n   756\u2192     *     <li>The record set has sat in the accumulator for at least lingerMs milliseconds</li>\n   757\u2192     *     <li>The accumulator is out of memory and threads are blocking waiting for data (in this case all partitions\n   758\u2192     *     are immediately considered ready).</li>\n   759\u2192     *     <li>The accumulator has been closed</li>\n   760\u2192     * </ul>\n   761\u2192     * </ol>\n   762\u2192     */\n   763\u2192    public ReadyCheckResult ready(MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot, long nowMs) {\n   764\u2192        Set<Node> readyNodes = new HashSet<>();\n   765\u2192        long nextReadyCheckDelayMs = Long.MAX_VALUE;\n   766\u2192        Set<String> unknownLeaderTopics = new HashSet<>();\n   767\u2192        // Go topic by topic so that we can get queue sizes for partitions in a topic and calculate\n   768\u2192        // cumulative frequency table (used in partitioner).\n   769\u2192        for (Map.Entry<String, TopicInfo> topicInfoEntry : this.topicInfoMap.entrySet()) {\n   770\u2192            final String topic = topicInfoEntry.getKey();\n   771\u2192            nextReadyCheckDelayMs = partitionReady(metadataSnapshot, nowMs, topic, topicInfoEntry.getValue(), nextReadyCheckDelayMs, readyNodes, unknownLeaderTopics);\n   772\u2192        }\n   773\u2192        return new ReadyCheckResult(readyNodes, nextReadyCheckDelayMs, unknownLeaderTopics);\n   774\u2192    }\n   775\u2192\n   776\u2192    /**\n   777\u2192     * Check whether there are any batches which haven't been drained\n   778\u2192     */\n   779\u2192    public boolean hasUndrained() {\n   780\u2192        for (TopicInfo topicInfo : topicInfoMap.values()) {\n   781\u2192            for (Deque<ProducerBatch> deque : topicInfo.batches.values()) {\n   782\u2192                synchronized (deque) {\n   783\u2192                    if (!deque.isEmpty())\n   784\u2192                        return true;\n   785\u2192                }\n   786\u2192            }\n   787\u2192        }\n   788\u2192        return false;\n   789\u2192    }\n   790\u2192\n   791\u2192    private boolean shouldBackoff(boolean hasLeaderChanged, final ProducerBatch batch, final long waitedTimeMs) {\n   792\u2192        boolean shouldWaitMore = batch.attempts() > 0 && waitedTimeMs < retryBackoff.backoff(batch.attempts() - 1);\n   793\u2192        boolean shouldBackoff = !hasLeaderChanged && shouldWaitMore;\n   794\u2192        if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\n   795\u2192            if (shouldBackoff) {\n   796\u2192                log.trace(\n   797\u2192                    \"For {}, will backoff\", batch);\n   798\u2192            } else {\n   799\u2192                log.trace(\n   800\u2192                    \"For {}, will not backoff, shouldWaitMore {}, hasLeaderChanged {}\", batch,\n   801\u2192                    shouldWaitMore, hasLeaderChanged);\n   802\u2192            }\n   803\u2192        } else if (log.isDebugEnabled() && hasLeaderChanged) {\n   804\u2192            // Add less-verbose log at DEBUG.\n   805\u2192            log.debug(\"For {}, leader has changed, hence skipping backoff.\", batch);\n   806\u2192        }\n   807\u2192        return shouldBackoff;\n   808\u2192    }\n   809\u2192\n   810\u2192    private boolean shouldStopDrainBatchesForPartition(ProducerBatch first, TopicPartition tp) {\n   811\u2192        ProducerIdAndEpoch producerIdAndEpoch;\n   812\u2192        if (transactionManager != null) {\n   813\u2192            if (!transactionManager.isSendToPartitionAllowed(tp))\n   814\u2192                return true;\n   815\u2192\n   816\u2192            producerIdAndEpoch = transactionManager.producerIdAndEpoch();\n   817\u2192            if (!producerIdAndEpoch.isValid())\n   818\u2192                // we cannot send the batch until we have refreshed the producer id\n   819\u2192                return true;\n   820\u2192\n   821\u2192            if (!first.hasSequence()) {\n   822\u2192                if (transactionManager.hasInflightBatches(tp) && transactionManager.hasStaleProducerIdAndEpoch(tp)) {\n   823\u2192                    // Don't drain any new batches while the partition has in-flight batches with a different epoch\n   824\u2192                    // and/or producer ID. Otherwise, a batch with a new epoch and sequence number\n   825\u2192                    // 0 could be written before earlier batches complete, which would cause out of sequence errors\n   826\u2192                    return true;\n   827\u2192                }\n   828\u2192\n   829\u2192                if (transactionManager.hasUnresolvedSequence(first.topicPartition))\n   830\u2192                    // Don't drain any new batches while the state of previous sequence numbers\n   831\u2192                    // is unknown. The previous batches would be unknown if they were aborted\n   832\u2192                    // on the client after being sent to the broker at least once.\n   833\u2192                    return true;\n   834\u2192            }\n   835\u2192\n   836\u2192            int firstInFlightSequence = transactionManager.firstInFlightSequence(first.topicPartition);\n   837\u2192            // If the queued batch already has an assigned sequence, then it is being retried.\n   838\u2192            // In this case, we wait until the next immediate batch is ready and drain that.\n   839\u2192            // We only move on when the next in line batch is complete (either successfully or due to\n   840\u2192            // a fatal broker error). This effectively reduces our in flight request count to 1.\n   841\u2192            return firstInFlightSequence != RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE && first.hasSequence()\n   842\u2192                    && first.baseSequence() != firstInFlightSequence;\n   843\u2192        }\n   844\u2192        return false;\n   845\u2192    }\n   846\u2192\n   847\u2192    private List<ProducerBatch> drainBatchesForOneNode(MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot, Node node, int maxSize, long now) {\n   848\u2192        int size = 0;\n   849\u2192        List<PartitionInfo> parts = metadataSnapshot.cluster().partitionsForNode(node.id());\n   850\u2192        List<ProducerBatch> ready = new ArrayList<>();\n   851\u2192        if (parts.isEmpty())\n   852\u2192            return ready;\n   853\u2192        /* to make starvation less likely each node has it's own drainIndex */\n   854\u2192        int drainIndex = getDrainIndex(node.idString());\n   855\u2192        int start = drainIndex = drainIndex % parts.size();\n   856\u2192        do {\n   857\u2192            PartitionInfo part = parts.get(drainIndex);\n   858\u2192\n   859\u2192            TopicPartition tp = new TopicPartition(part.topic(), part.partition());\n   860\u2192            updateDrainIndex(node.idString(), drainIndex);\n   861\u2192            drainIndex = (drainIndex + 1) % parts.size();\n   862\u2192            // Only proceed if the partition has no in-flight batches.\n   863\u2192            if (isMuted(tp))\n   864\u2192                continue;\n   865\u2192            Deque<ProducerBatch> deque = getDeque(tp);\n   866\u2192            if (deque == null)\n   867\u2192                continue;\n   868\u2192\n   869\u2192            OptionalInt leaderEpoch = metadataSnapshot.leaderEpochFor(tp);\n   870\u2192\n   871\u2192            final ProducerBatch batch;\n   872\u2192            synchronized (deque) {\n   873\u2192                // invariant: !isMuted(tp,now) && deque != null\n   874\u2192                ProducerBatch first = deque.peekFirst();\n   875\u2192                if (first == null)\n   876\u2192                    continue;\n   877\u2192\n   878\u2192                // first != null\n   879\u2192                // Only drain the batch if it is not during backoff period.\n   880\u2192                first.maybeUpdateLeaderEpoch(leaderEpoch);\n   881\u2192                if (shouldBackoff(first.hasLeaderChangedForTheOngoingRetry(), first, first.waitedTimeMs(now)))\n   882\u2192 ## Sample Code Changes

### Example 1: Main Class Definition (BatchAccumulator.java)

**Before:**
```java
public class RecordAccumulator {
    private final LogContext logContext;
    private final Logger log;
    // ... class body ...
    public static final class RecordAppendResult { ... }
    public static final class ReadyCheckResult { ... }
}
```

**After:**
```java
public class BatchAccumulator {
    private final LogContext logContext;
    private final Logger log;
    // ... class body ...
    public static final class RecordAppendResult { ... }
    public static final class ReadyCheckResult { ... }
}
```

### Example 2: KafkaProducer.java Usage

**Before:**
```java
import org.apache.kafka.clients.producer.internals.RecordAccumulator;

public class KafkaProducer {
    private final RecordAccumulator accumulator;

    this.accumulator = new RecordAccumulator(logContext, ...);
    RecordAccumulator.RecordAppendResult result = accumulator.append(...);
}
```

**After:**
```java
import org.apache.kafka.clients.producer.internals.BatchAccumulator;

public class KafkaProducer {
    private final BatchAccumulator accumulator;

    this.accumulator = new BatchAccumulator(logContext, ...);
    BatchAccumulator.RecordAppendResult result = accumulator.append(...);
}
```

### Example 3: Sender.java Usage

**Before:**
```java
private final RecordAccumulator accumulator;

RecordAccumulator.ReadyCheckResult result = this.accumulator.ready(metadataSnapshot, now);
```

**After:**
```java
private final BatchAccumulator accumulator;

BatchAccumulator.ReadyCheckResult result = this.accumulator.ready(metadataSnapshot, now);
```

The RecordAccumulator class manages per-partition queues of ProducerBatch 
objects. Its core data structure is ConcurrentMap<TopicPartition, Deque<ProducerBatch>>,
and key methods (ready(), drain(), append()) operate at batch granularity.
Renaming to BatchAccumulator better reflects this responsibility.
